FROM (
    SELECT `t`.`shipStatus`, `t`.`tripID` IS NOT NULL AND (`t`.`tripID` <> '') AS `HasTripId`
    FROM `tblOrders` AS `t`
    WHERE (`t`.`isDeleted` IS NULL) OR NOT (`t`.`isDeleted`)
) AS `t0`
GROUP BY `t0`.`shipStatus`, `t0`.`HasTripId`
